    /* Added Deferred and the code below to fix menu render problem */
    $("#menu1").kendoMenu();

    $(document).click(function (event) {
        var isMenuClick = false;
        if (!($(event.target).hasClass("menuheader") || $(event.target).hasClass("menuheaderrollover") || $(event.target).hasClass("k-icon k-i-arrow-s")))
        {
            for (var i = 0; i &lt; 8; i++)
            {
                if ($(event.target).closest('#menudropdown' + i).length)
                {
                    isMenuClick = true;
                    break;
                }
            }
            if (!isMenuClick)
            {
                hideopendropdowns(8);
            }
        }
    });
</script>

<script>
    var isFromLoad = false;
    function VendorComboChange() { }
    function DeductionGroupComboChange() { }
    function W2BoxNumberComboChange() {
        var W2BoxNumberDropdownlist = $("#W2BoxNumber").data("kendoDropDownList");
        var W2SubCodeDropdownlist = $("#W2SubCode").data("kendoDropDownList");
        var W2BoxNumber = $("#W2BoxNumber").val();

        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollDeduction/GetW2SubCodeList',
            cache: false,
            data: { selectedW2BoxNumber: W2BoxNumber },
            dataType: 'JSON',
            success: function (result) {
                //debugger;
                if (typeof result !== "undefined" &amp;&amp; result != null) {
                    // updating dropdownlist datasource
                    W2SubCodeDropdownlist.setDataSource(result);
                    W2SubCodeDropdownlist.refresh();

                }
            }
        });

        if (!(W2BoxNumber == '11' || W2BoxNumber == '12' || W2BoxNumber == '13' || W2BoxNumber == '14' || W2BoxNumber == '15')) {
            W2SubCodeDropdownlist.readonly();
        }
        else {
            W2SubCodeDropdownlist.readonly(false);
        }
    }

    function W2SubCodeComboChange() {

    }
    function BasedOnComboChange() { }
    function EmployeeLiabElementValueComboChange() { }
    function EmployerExpElementValueComboChange() { }
    function EmployerLiabElementValueComboChange() { }

    function SetIncludeOTDisabled() {
        $("input:radio[name=IncludeOT]").each(function () {
            this.disabled = true;
        });
    }
    function SetIncludeOTEnabled() {
        $("input:radio[name=IncludeOT]").each(function () {
            this.disabled = false;
        });
    }
    function GetDeductOrder() {

        var deductOrder = "";
        $("input:radio[name=DeductionOrder]").each(function () {
            //debugger;
            if (this.checked)
                deductOrder = this.value;
        });

        var data = { deductOrder: deductOrder };
        return data;
    }
    function SetCalculationMethodEnabled() {
        var deductType = "";
        $("input:radio[name=DeductionType]").each(function () {
            // debugger;
            if (this.checked)
                deductType = this.value;
        });

        if (deductType == "FTE Benefit") {
            //set calculatemethod to fixed and disable all calculation method
            var calculationMethod = '';
            $("input:radio[name=CalculationMethod]").each(function () {
                //debugger;
                calculationMethod = this.value;
                if (calculationMethod == "Fixed Amount") {
                    this.checked = true;
                    $('#CalcMethod').val('Fixed Amount');
                }
                this.disabled = true;
            });
        }
        else {
            $("input:radio[name=CalculationMethod]").each(function () {
                this.disabled = false;
            });
        }
    }

    function SetAmountPercentageVisible() {
        var calculationMethod = '';
        $("input:radio[name=CalculationMethod]").each(function () {
            if (this.checked)
                calculationMethod = this.value;
        });
        //debugger;
        //if calculation method is fixed then hide employee and employer sections period percentage text boxes.
        if (calculationMethod == "Fixed Amount") {
            $("#lblEmployeePeriodAmount").show();
            $("#EmployeePeriodAmount").data("kendoNumericTextBox").wrapper.show();
            $("#lblEmployerPeriodAmount").show();
            $("#EmployerPeriodAmount").data("kendoNumericTextBox").wrapper.show();

            $("#lblEmployeePeriodPercent").hide();
            $("#EmployeePeriodPercent").data("kendoNumericTextBox").wrapper.hide();
            $("#lblEmployerPeriodPercent").hide();
            $("#EmployerPeriodPercent").data("kendoNumericTextBox").wrapper.hide();

            // set percentage controls to zero or you will get 50052 sql error when saving.
            var employeePeriodPercent = $("#EmployeePeriodPercent").data("kendoNumericTextBox").value();
            if (employeePeriodPercent &gt; 0) {
                document.getElementById("EmployeePeriodPercent").value = "";
            }
            var employerPeriodPercent = $("#EmployerPeriodPercent").data("kendoNumericTextBox").value();
            if (employerPeriodPercent &gt; 0) {
                document.getElementById("EmployerPeriodPercent").value = "";
            }

        }
        else if (calculationMethod == "Percentage") {
            //else if calculation method is percentage then hide employee and employer sections period amount text boxes

            $("#lblEmployeePeriodAmount").hide();
            $("#EmployeePeriodAmount").data("kendoNumericTextBox").wrapper.hide();
            $("#lblEmployerPeriodAmount").hide();
            $("#EmployerPeriodAmount").data("kendoNumericTextBox").wrapper.hide();

            $("#lblEmployeePeriodPercent").show();
            $("#EmployeePeriodPercent").data("kendoNumericTextBox").wrapper.show();
            $("#lblEmployerPeriodPercent").show();
            $("#EmployerPeriodPercent").data("kendoNumericTextBox").wrapper.show();

            // set amount to zero or you will get 50052 sql error when saving.
            var EmployeePeriodAmount = $("#EmployeePeriodAmount").data("kendoNumericTextBox").value();
            if (EmployeePeriodAmount &gt; 0) {
                document.getElementById("EmployeePeriodAmount").value = "";
            }
            var EmployerPeriodAmount = $("#EmployerPeriodAmount").data("kendoNumericTextBox").value();
            if (EmployerPeriodAmount &gt; 0) {
                document.getElementById("EmployerPeriodAmount").value = "";
            }

        }

    }

    function SetBasedOnVisible() {
        var calculationMethod = '';
        $("input:radio[name=CalculationMethod]").each(function () {
            if (this.checked)
                calculationMethod = this.value;
        })

        //if CalculationMethod is Fixed || CalculationMethod is DirectDeposit then hide based on field else show
        if (calculationMethod == "Fixed Amount" || calculationMethod == "Direct Deposit") {
            $("#lblBasedOn").hide();
            $("#BasedOn").data("kendoDropDownList").wrapper.hide();
        }
        else {
            $("#lblBasedOn").show();
            $("#BasedOn").data("kendoDropDownList").wrapper.show();
        }
    }

    function LoadBasedOnCombo() {
        $.ajax({
            url: '/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollDeduction/GetBasedOnList',
            cache: false,
            data: GetDeductOrder(),
            dataType: 'JSON',
            success: function (result) {
                //debugger;
                if (typeof result !== "undefined" &amp;&amp; result != null) {
                    // updating dropdownlist datasource
                    var ddl = $("#BasedOn").data("kendoDropDownList");
                    ddl.setDataSource(result);
                    ddl.refresh();

                }
            }
        });
    }
    function OnDeductionTypeSelection() {
        SetCalculationMethodEnabled();
        OnCalculationMethodSelection();
    }

    function OnCalculationMethodSelection() {
        SetAmountPercentageVisible();
        SetBasedOnVisible();
    }

    function OnDeductOrderSelection() {
        LoadBasedOnCombo();
        if (!isFromLoad) {
            if ($("#PayrollDeductionOrder_PreSSN").is(":checked") || $("#PayrollDeductionOrder_PreTax").is(":checked")) {
                $("#IsStateTaxableIncomeAffected").prop("checked", true);
            }
            else if ($("#PayrollDeductionOrder_PostTax").is(":checked")) {
                $("#IsStateTaxableIncomeAffected").prop("checked", false);
            }

            if ('0' != '0') {
                var form = $("#FormPayrollDeduction");
                $.ajax({
                    type: "POST",
                    url: form.attr('action'),
                    data: form.serialize(),
                    success: function (result) {
                    }
                });
            }

        }
    }
    function OnDefaultChange() {
        //debugger;
        if ($('#Default').is(":checked")) {
            $('#DeductionGroupList').data("kendoMultiSelect").enable(false);
        }
        else {
            $('#DeductionGroupList').data("kendoMultiSelect").enable(true);
        }
    }

    function ReturnFromIncludeMasterPositionPopup() {

    }

    function OpenIncludeMasterPositionpopup() {
        var finsWindow = FINSWindow.FinsWindowManager.CreateFINSWindowObject("popupwindowIncludeMasterPosition")
                        .SetContent({
                            url: "/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollDeduction/IncludeMasterPosition",
                            type: "POST",
                            data: $("#FormPayrollDeduction").serialize()
                        })
        .SetWidth(690)
        .SetHeight(400)
        .SetTitle('Jobs/Addenda')
        .SetonDeactivate(function () { ReturnFromIncludeMasterPositionPopup(); })
        finsWindow.CreateWindow(true);
    }
    function SetJobsDisabled() {
        var jobList = $('#JobList');
        $('#btnOpenMasterPositionList').remove();
        jobList.val("All");
    }
    function OverrideOT() {
        $('#PayrollIncludeOT_YesAllPay').prop('checked', true);
        $('#IncOT').val('Yes (All Pay)');
        SetIncludeOTDisabled();
    }

    $(document).on('click', '#btnOpenMasterPositionList', function () {
        if ('' == 'Percentage' || 'False') {
            OpenIncludeMasterPositionpopup();
        }
    });
    $('#PayrollDeductionType_Deduction').click(function () { OnDeductionTypeSelection(); });
    $('#PayrollDeductionType_Benefit').click(function () { OnDeductionTypeSelection(); });
    $('#PayrollDeductionType_TaxableBenefit').click(function () { OnDeductionTypeSelection(); });
    $('#PayrollDeductionType_FTEBenefit').click(function () {
        OnDeductionTypeSelection();
        $('#PayrollCalculationMethod_FixedAmount').prop('checked', true);
        OverrideOT();
        SetJobsDisabled();
    });

    $('#PayrollCalculationMethod_FixedAmount').click(function () {
        OverrideOT();
        OnCalculationMethodSelection();
        $('#CalcMethod').val('Fixed Amount');
        SetJobsDisabled();
    });
    $('#PayrollCalculationMethod_Percentage').click(function () {
        var includeOTAllPay = $('#PayrollIncludeOT_YesAllPay');
        OnCalculationMethodSelection();
        $('#CalcMethod').val('Percentage');
        SetIncludeOTEnabled();
        if (!$('#btnOpenMasterPositionList').length) {
            $('#JobList').after("&lt;a id='btnOpenMasterPositionList' class='k-button'&gt;...&lt;/a&gt;")
        }
        includeOTAllPay.prop('checked', true);
    });
    $('#PayrollCalculationMethod_Withholding').click(function () {
        OnCalculationMethodSelection();
        $('#CalcMethod').val('Withholding');
        SetIncludeOTDisabled();
        SetJobsDisabled();
    });
    $('#PayrollCalculationMethod_DirectDeposit').click(function () {
        OnCalculationMethodSelection();
        $('#CalcMethod').val('Direct Deposit');
        SetIncludeOTDisabled();
        SetJobsDisabled();
    });

    $('#PayrollDeductionOrder_PreSSN').click(function () {
        isFromLoad = false;
        OnDeductOrderSelection();
    });
    $('#PayrollDeductionOrder_PreTax').click(function () {
        isFromLoad = false;
        OnDeductOrderSelection();
    });
    $('#PayrollDeductionOrder_Tax').click(function () {
        isFromLoad = false;
        OnDeductOrderSelection();
    });
    $('#PayrollDeductionOrder_PostTax').click(function () {
        isFromLoad = false;
        OnDeductOrderSelection();
    });

    $("#btnSave__PayrollDeduction").click(function () {

        var W2BoxNumber = $("#W2BoxNumber").val();
        var W2SubCode = $("#W2SubCode").val();
        var SecondaryW2BoxNumber = $("#SecondaryW2BoxNumber").val();
        var SecondaryW2SubCode = $("#SecondaryW2SubCode").val();
        var validationMessage = '';

        if ((W2BoxNumber == '12' || W2BoxNumber == '13' || W2BoxNumber == '14' || W2BoxNumber == '15') &amp;&amp; (typeof W2SubCode == 'undefined' || W2SubCode == '' || W2SubCode == null)) {
            validationMessage += 'W-2 Sub Code cannot be blank if the W-2 Box No. is 12, 13, 14, or 15.' + '&lt;br /&gt;' + '&lt;br /&gt;';
        }
        if (SecondaryW2BoxNumber != '' &amp;&amp; SecondaryW2SubCode == '') {
            validationMessage += 'Secondary W-2 Sub Code cannot be blank if the Secondary W-2 Box No. is specified.' + '&lt;br /&gt;';
        }

        if (validationMessage != '') {
            ShowAjaxMessage(validationMessage, "error");
            return;
        }

        $('#IsLastRecord').val(true);
        $("#FormPayrollDeduction").submit();

    });

    $("#btnSaveAndNext__PayrollDeduction").click(function () {

        var W2BoxNumber = $("#W2BoxNumber").val();
        var W2SubCode = $("#W2SubCode").val();
        var SecondaryW2BoxNumber = $("#SecondaryW2BoxNumber").val();
        var SecondaryW2SubCode = $("#SecondaryW2SubCode").val();
        var validationMessage = '';

        if ((W2BoxNumber == '12' || W2BoxNumber == '13' || W2BoxNumber == '14' || W2BoxNumber == '15') &amp;&amp; (typeof W2SubCode == 'undefined' || W2SubCode == '' || W2SubCode == null)) {
            validationMessage += 'W-2 Sub Code cannot be blank if the W-2 Box No. is 12, 13, 14, or 15.' + '&lt;br /&gt;' + '&lt;br /&gt;';
        }
        if (SecondaryW2BoxNumber != '' &amp;&amp; SecondaryW2SubCode == '') {
            validationMessage += 'Secondary W-2 Sub Code cannot be blank if the Secondary W-2 Box No. is specified.' + '&lt;br /&gt;';
        }

        if (validationMessage != '') {
            ShowAjaxMessage(validationMessage, "error");
            return;
        }

        $("#FormPayrollDeduction").submit();

    });

    $('#Default').on("click", OnDefaultChange);

    $(document).ready(function () {
        isFromLoad = true;
        OnDeductionTypeSelection(); OnDeductOrderSelection(); OnDefaultChange();
        var deductionId = "0";
        var deductionOrder = '';

        var isFullDeductionAccountMaskAllowed = 'False';

        if ('' === 'Fixed Amount' || '' === 'Enabled') {
            SetIncludeOTDisabled();
        }

        if (deductionOrder == "Tax") {
            $('input[name=DeductionOrder]').attr("disabled", true);
        }
        var vendorDropdownlist = $("#VendorId").data("kendoComboBox");

        var prioNumerictextbox = $("#Priority").data("kendoNumericTextBox");
        var EmployeePeriodAmountText = $("#EmployeePeriodAmount").data("kendoNumericTextBox");
        var EmployeeMonthlyCapText = $("#EmployeeMonthlyCap").data("kendoNumericTextBox");
        var EmployeeYearlyCapText = $("#EmployeeYearlyCap").data("kendoNumericTextBox");
        var EmployeeMultiYearCapText = $("#EmployeeMultiYearCap").data("kendoNumericTextBox");
        var PeriodPercentCapText = $("#PeriodPercentCap").data("kendoNumericTextBox");
        var EmployerPeriodAmountText = $("#EmployerPeriodAmount").data("kendoNumericTextBox");
        var EmployerMonthlyCapText = $("#EmployerMonthlyCap").data("kendoNumericTextBox");
        var EmployerYearlyCapText = $("#EmployerYearlyCap").data("kendoNumericTextBox");

        //var DGmultiSelect = $("#DeductionGroup").data("kendoMultiSelect");
        if ('' == "Enabled" || '' == 'Withholding' || '' == 'Direct Deposit') {
            $('#DeductionName').attr('readonly', true);
            $('#Comment').attr('readonly', true);
            $('input[name=DeductionType]').attr("disabled", true);
            $('input[name=CalculationMethod]').attr("disabled", true);
            $('input[name=DeductionOrder]').attr("disabled", true);
            $('input[name=Default]').attr("disabled", true);
            $('input[name=Is125DeductionBool]').attr("disabled", true);
            $('input[name=Variable]').attr("disabled", true);
            $('input[name=AnnualCapType]').attr("disabled", true);
            $('input[name=Retirement]').attr("disabled", true);
            vendorDropdownlist.readonly();
            prioNumerictextbox.readonly();
            //DGmultiSelect.readonly();
            $('#EmployeeLiabAccountMask').attr('readonly', true);
            $('#EmployerExpAccountMask').attr('readonly', true);
            $('#EmployerLiabAccountMask').attr('readonly', true);

            $('input[name=IsStateTaxableIncomeAffected]').attr("disabled", true);
            $('input[name=IsDispIncomeAffected]').attr("disabled", true);
            EmployeePeriodAmountText.readonly();
            EmployeeMonthlyCapText.readonly();
            EmployeeYearlyCapText.readonly();
            EmployeeMultiYearCapText.readonly();
            PeriodPercentCapText.readonly();
            EmployerPeriodAmountText.readonly();
            EmployerMonthlyCapText.readonly();
            EmployerYearlyCapText.readonly();
            var EmployerExpDropdownlist = $("#EmployerExpElementValueId").data("kendoDropDownList");
            var EmployeeLiabElementValueDropdownlist = $("#EmployeeLiabElementValueId").data("kendoDropDownList");
            var EmployerLiabElementValueDropdownlist = $("#EmployerLiabElementValueId").data("kendoDropDownList");
            var EmployeePeriodPercentText = $("#EmployeePeriodPercent").data("kendoNumericTextBox");
            var EmployerPeriodPercentText = $("#EmployerPeriodPercent").data("kendoNumericTextBox");
            var BasedOnDropdownlist = $("#BasedOn").data("kendoDropDownList");
            EmployerExpDropdownlist.readonly();
            EmployeeLiabElementValueDropdownlist.readonly();
            EmployerLiabElementValueDropdownlist.readonly();
            EmployeePeriodPercentText.readonly();
            EmployerPeriodPercentText.readonly();
            BasedOnDropdownlist.readonly();
        }
        else {
            $('#DeductionName').attr('readonly', false);
            $('#Comment').attr('readonly', false);
            $('input[name=DeductionType]').attr("disabled", false);
            $('input[name=CalculationMethod]').attr("disabled", false);
            $('input[name=DeductionOrder]').attr("disabled", false);
            $('input[name=Default]').attr("disabled", false);
            $('input[name=Is125DeductionBool]').attr("disabled", false);
            $('input[name=Variable]').attr("disabled", false);
            $('input[name=AnnualCapType]').attr("disabled", false);
            $('input[name=Retirement]').attr("disabled", false);
            vendorDropdownlist.readonly(false);
            prioNumerictextbox.readonly(false);
            //DGmultiSelect.readonly(false);
            $('#EmployeeLiabAccountMask').attr('readonly', false);
            $('#EmployerExpAccountMask').attr('readonly', false);
            $('#EmployerLiabAccountMask').attr('readonly', false);
            $('input[name=IsStateTaxableIncomeAffected]').attr("disabled", false);
            $('input[name=IsDispIncomeAffected]').attr("disabled", false);
            EmployeePeriodAmountText.readonly(false);
            EmployeeMonthlyCapText.readonly(false);
            EmployeeYearlyCapText.readonly(false);
            EmployeeMultiYearCapText.readonly(false);
            PeriodPercentCapText.readonly(false);
            EmployerPeriodAmountText.readonly(false);
            EmployerMonthlyCapText.readonly(false);
            EmployerYearlyCapText.readonly(false);
            var EmployerExpDropdownlist = $("#EmployerExpElementValueId").data("kendoDropDownList");
            var EmployeeLiabElementValueDropdownlist = $("#EmployeeLiabElementValueId").data("kendoDropDownList");
            var EmployerLiabElementValueDropdownlist = $("#EmployerLiabElementValueId").data("kendoDropDownList");
            EmployerExpDropdownlist.readonly(false);
            EmployeeLiabElementValueDropdownlist.readonly(false);
            EmployerLiabElementValueDropdownlist.readonly(false);
            var EmployeePeriodPercentText = $("#EmployeePeriodPercent").data("kendoNumericTextBox");
            var EmployerPeriodPercentText = $("#EmployerPeriodPercent").data("kendoNumericTextBox");
            var BasedOnDropdownlist = $("#BasedOn").data("kendoDropDownList");
            EmployeePeriodPercentText.readonly(false);
            EmployerPeriodPercentText.readonly(false);
            BasedOnDropdownlist.readonly(false);
        }
        var W2BoxNumberDropdownlist = $("#W2BoxNumber").data("kendoDropDownList");
        var SecondaryW2BoxNumberDropdownlist = $("#SecondaryW2BoxNumber").data("kendoDropDownList");
        var W2SubCodeDropdownlist = $("#W2SubCode").data("kendoDropDownList");
        var SecondaryW2SubCodeDropdownlist = $("#SecondaryW2SubCode").data("kendoDropDownList");

        if (('' == 'Withholding' || '' == 'Direct Deposit') &amp;&amp; '' == "Disabled") {
            $('input[name=IsRollover]').attr("disabled", true);
            W2BoxNumberDropdownlist.readonly();
            W2SubCodeDropdownlist.readonly();
            SecondaryW2BoxNumberDropdownlist.readonly();
            SecondaryW2SubCodeDropdownlist.readonly();
            vendorDropdownlist.readonly(false);
            $('#EmployeeLiabAccountMask').attr('readonly', false);
            $('#EmployerExpAccountMask').attr('readonly', false);
            $('#EmployerLiabAccountMask').attr('readonly', false);
            var EmployeeLiabElementValueDropdownlist = $("#EmployeeLiabElementValueId").data("kendoDropDownList");
            var EmployerLiabElementValueDropdownlist = $("#EmployerLiabElementValueId").data("kendoDropDownList");
            var EmployerExpElementValueDropDownlist = $("#EmployerExpElementValueId").data("kendoDropDownList");
            EmployerExpElementValueDropDownlist.readonly(false);
            EmployeeLiabElementValueDropdownlist.readonly(false);
            EmployerLiabElementValueDropdownlist.readonly(false);
        }
        else {
            $('input[name=IsRollover]').attr("disabled", false);
            W2BoxNumberComboChange();
            SecondaryW2BoxNumberDropdownlist.readonly(false);
            SecondaryW2SubCodeDropdownlist.readonly(false);
        }

        //debugger;

        if ('' == "FTE Benefit"){
            SetCalculationMethodEnabled();
        }
        if (isFullDeductionAccountMaskAllowed == 'True') {
            $("#EmployerExpAccountMask").show();
            $('label[for="EmployerExpAccountMask"]').show();

            $("#EmployeeLiabAccountMask").show();
            $('label[for="EmployeeLiabAccountMask"]').show();

            $("#EmployerLiabAccountMask").show();
            $('label[for="EmployerLiabAccountMask"]').show();

            $("#EmployeeLiabElementValueId").closest(".k-widget").hide();
            $('label[for="EmployeeLiabElementValueId"]').hide();

            $("#EmployerLiabElementValueId").closest(".k-widget").hide();
            $('label[for="EmployerLiabElementValueId"]').hide();

            $("#EmployerExpElementValueId").closest(".k-widget").hide();
            $('label[for="EmployerExpElementValueId"]').hide();

        }
        else {
            $("#EmployerExpAccountMask").hide();
            $('label[for="EmployerExpAccountMask"]').hide();

            $("#EmployeeLiabAccountMask").hide();
            $('label[for="EmployeeLiabAccountMask"]').hide();

            $("#EmployerLiabAccountMask").hide();
            $('label[for="EmployerLiabAccountMask"]').hide();

            $("#EmployerLiabElementValueId").closest(".k-widget").show();
            $('label[for="EmployerLiabElementValueId"]').show();

            $("#EmployeeLiabElementValueId").closest(".k-widget").show();
            $('label[for="EmployeeLiabElementValueId"]').show();

            $("#EmployerExpElementValueId").closest(".k-widget").show();
            $('label[for="EmployerExpElementValueId"]').show();
        }

    });

            selectedSecondaryW2BoxNumber: $("#SecondaryW2BoxNumber").val()
        }

    }

        return {
            selectedW2BoxNumber: $("#W2BoxNumber").val()
        }

    <script type="text/javascript">

        $(document).click(function (event) {

            if (event.target.id == "btnMoreButtons" || event.target.parentNode.id == "btnMoreButtons") {
                event.preventDefault();
                showHideMoreButtons();
            }
            else {
                if ($('#dvMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                    document.getElementById("dvMoreButtons").style.display = "none";
                }
            }
            if (event.target.classList.contains('btnDetailMoreButtons') || (event.target.parentNode != null &amp;&amp; event.target.parentNode.classList != null &amp;&amp; event.target.parentNode.classList.contains("btnDetailMoreButtons"))) {
                event.preventDefault();
                var id = event.target.id;
                if (event.target.id == "") {
                    id = event.target.parentNode.id;
                }
                showHideDetailMoreButtons(id);
            }
            else {
                if ($('.dvDetailMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                    $('.dvDetailMoreButtons').each(function () {
                        $(this).css('display', 'none');
                    });
                }
            }
        });

        $(window).scroll(function () {
            if ($('#dvMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                ShowMoreMenu();
            }
            if ($('.dvDetailMoreButtons').is(':visible')) {
                $('.dvDetailMoreButtons').each(function () {
                    if ($(this).css('display') != 'none') {
                        ShowDetailMoreMenu(this.id);
                    }
                });
            }
        });

        $(window).resize(function () {
            ResetDivMoreButtonOnResize();
        });

        var _jobQueueNotificationTimer;

        function StartJobQueueNotifications() {
            if (_jobQueueNotificationTimer == null)
                CheckJobQueueNotifications('/QAAutom/Home/CheckJobQueueStatus');
        }

        function DismissJobQueueNotification(jobQueueID) {
            $.ajax({
                cache: false,
                async: false,
                data: { jobQueueID: jobQueueID },
                dataType: "json",
                url: '/QAAutom/Payroll/PayrollDeduction/DismissJobQueueStatus',
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result.Message != "") {
                        FINSUI.FINSUINotifications.JobQueueNotification().ShowJobQueueNotification(result.TempData, result.Message)
                    } else {
                        FINSUI.FINSUINotifications.JobQueueNotification().hide();
                    }
                }
            });
        }
    </script>


<script>
    $(document).ready(function () {
        FINSUI.FINSUIElement.setAptaFundBaseURL("/QAAutom/controller/action", true);
        

        if ('Detail' == "Detail") {
            doStickyButtons();
        }
        registerFINSComboBoxEvents();
        $("body").find("input, textarea, select, span[role=listbox]").filter(":visible:not([disabled]):not([readonly]):not([tabindex=-1]):first").focus();

    });

    function doStickyButtons() {
        var sticky_button_offset_top = $('#menuhr').offset().top;

        // our function that decides weather the navigation bar should have "fixed" css position or not.
        var sticky_button_navigation = function () {
            var scroll_top = $(window).scrollTop(); // our current vertical position from the top
            var screenwidth = $(window).width();
            var buttonswidth = $('#actionbuttons').width();
            var buttonsheight = $('#actionbuttons').height();

            // if we've scrolled more than the navigation, change its position to fixed to stick to top,
            // otherwise change it back to relative
            if (scroll_top &gt; sticky_button_offset_top) {
                $('#menuhr').css({ 'position': 'fixed', 'top': 0, 'left': 40, 'z-index': 11, 'width': (screenwidth - 80) });
                $('#actionbuttons').css({ 'position': 'fixed', 'top': 10, 'right': 48, 'z-index': 12, 'width': buttonswidth });
                $('#actionbuttonswrapper').css({ 'height': buttonsheight });
            } else {
                $('#menuhr').removeAttr('style');
                $('#actionbuttons').removeAttr('style');
                $('#actionbuttonswrapper').removeAttr('style');
            }
        };

        // run our function on load
        sticky_button_navigation();

        // and run it again every time you scroll
        $(window).scroll(function () {
            sticky_button_navigation();
        });
    }

    
    function registerFINSComboBoxEvents() {
        $('.FINSComboBox').each(function () {
            var kendoCombo = $(this).data("kendoComboBox");
            if (kendoCombo != null) {

                kendoCombo.bind("select", function (e) {
                    if (e.item != null) {
                        var dataItem = this.dataItem(e.item.index());
                        if (dataItem.Value == -999) {
                            e.preventDefault();
                        }
                    }

                }
               );

            }
        });
    }
